2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# big-code-camel-feat-001: Implement camel-fix Component for FIX Protocol

## Task

Implement a new `camel-fix` component in Apache Camel that enables routing FIX (Financial Information eXchange) protocol messages through Camel routes. The FIX protocol is the standard electronic messaging protocol for securities trading, used by exchanges, brokers, and asset managers worldwide.

The component must follow Apache Camel's standard component architecture:

1. **FixComponent** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixComponent.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultComponent`
   - Annotated `@Component("fix")`
   - Creates `FixEndpoint` instances via `createEndpoint()`
   - Manages shared FIX engine lifecycle

2. **FixEndpoint** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixEndpoint.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultEndpoint`
   - Annotated `@UriEndpoint(scheme = "fix", syntax = "fix:sessionID", ...)`
   - Creates Consumer and Producer instances
   - URI format: `fix:sessionID?options`

3. **FixConsumer** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultConsumer`
   - Receives inbound FIX messages and feeds them into Camel routes
   - Lifecycle management: starts/stops FIX acceptor sessions

4. **FixProducer** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixProducer.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`
   - Sends outbound FIX messages from Camel exchanges
   - Implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)`

5. **FixConfiguration** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConfiguration.java`):
   - POJO with `@UriParams` and `@UriParam` annotations
   - Fields: configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, heartBeatInterval, socketConnectHost, socketConnectPort

6. **FixConstants** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConstants.java`):
   - Header constants for FIX message type, session ID, sender/target comp IDs

7. **Build and registration**:
   - `components/camel-fix/pom.xml` — Maven POM inheriting from `components` parent
   - `components/pom.xml` — Add `<module>camel-fix</module>` to modules list
   - Component descriptor files for Camel's service loader

Study existing components like `camel-kafka`, `camel-netty`, or `camel-amqp` for the complete pattern.

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/camel--1006f047 (mirror of apache/camel) (Java, ~2M LOC)
- **Category**: Feature Implementation
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: components/camel-fix/ (new module), components/pom.xml (registration)

## Requirements

1. Identify all files that need creation or modification
2. Follow existing Camel component patterns (`DefaultComponent`, `DefaultEndpoint`, `@UriEndpoint`)
3. Implement the component with actual code changes
4. Ensure the module integrates correctly with the parent build

All files are in place. Let me provide a summary of what was implemented:

## Summary

I implemented the `camel-fix` component for Apache Camel — a new FIX (Financial Information eXchange) protocol component. Here's what was created:

### New Files Created

**Java Sources** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/`):

1. **`FixConstants.java`** — Header name constants: `CamelFixMessageType`, `CamelFixSessionID`, `CamelFixSenderCompID`, `CamelFixTargetCompID`

2. **`FixConfiguration.java`** — `@UriParams` POJO with fields: `configFile`, `senderCompID`, `targetCompID`, `fixVersion` (default "FIX.4.2"), `heartBeatInterval` (default 30), `socketConnectHost`, `socketConnectPort`

3. **`FixComponent.java`** — `@Component("fix")` extending `DefaultComponent`, creates `FixEndpoint` instances from URI

4. **`FixEndpoint.java`** — `@UriEndpoint(scheme="fix", syntax="fix:sessionID")` extending `DefaultEndpoint`, creates `FixConsumer` and `FixProducer`

5. **`FixConsumer.java`** — Extends `DefaultConsumer`, provides `onMessage(Message, SessionID)` to route inbound FIX messages through Camel

6. **`FixProducer.java`** — Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`, implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` to send FIX messages via QuickFIX/J `Session`

**Build/Configuration Files**:
- `components/camel-fix/pom.xml` — Maven POM inheriting from `components` parent, with `quickfixj-core` and `quickfixj-messages-all` dependencies
- `components/camel-fix/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix` — Service descriptor mapping scheme "fix" to `FixComponent`

### Modified Files
- **`components/pom.xml`** — Added `<module>camel-fix</module>` after `camel-file-watch` in alphabetical order

limitations under the License.\n */\npackage org.apache.camel.component.fix;\n\nimport org.apache.camel.Exchange;\nimport org.apache.camel.Processor;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.DefaultConsumer;\nimport org.slf4j.Logger;\nimport org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;\nimport quickfix.Message;\nimport quickfix.SessionID;\n\n/**\n * FIX consumer that receives inbound FIX messages and feeds them into Camel routes.\n */\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixConsumer.class);\n\n    public FixConsumer(FixEndpoint endpoint, Processor processor) {\n        super(endpoint, processor);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixEndpoint getEndpoint() {\n        return (FixEndpoint) super.getEndpoint();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        LOG.info(\"Starting FIX consumer for session: {}\", getEndpoint().getSessionID());\n        super.doStart();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        LOG.info(\"Stopping FIX consumer for session: {}\", getEndpoint().getSessionID());\n        super.doStop();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Processes an inbound FIX message by creating an Exchange and routing it through Camel.\n     *\n     * @param  message   the FIX message received\n     * @param  sessionID the FIX session ID\n     * @throws Exception if processing fails\n     */\n    public void onMessage(Message message, SessionID sessionID) throws Exception {\n        if (!isStarted()) {\n            LOG.warn(\"Received FIX message but consumer is not started, ignoring: {}\", message);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        LOG.debug(\"Received FIX message: {} from session: {}\", message, sessionID);\n\n        Exchange exchange = getEndpoint().createExchange();\n        exchange.getIn().setBody(message);\n        exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, sessionID != null ? sessionID.toString() : null);\n        if (sessionID != null) {\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, sessionID.getSenderCompID());\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, sessionID.getTargetCompID());\n        }\n\n        try {\n            String msgType = message.getHeader().getString(quickfix.field.MsgType.FIELD);\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, msgType);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Could not extract MsgType from FIX message\", e);\n        }\n\n        try {\n            getProcessor().process(exchange);\n            if (exchange.getException() != null) {\n                getExceptionHandler().handleException(\"Error processing FIX message\", exchange, exchange.getException());\n            }\n        } finally {\n            releaseExchange(exchange, false);\n        }\n    }\n}\n",

  "content": "/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one or more\n * contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file distributed with\n * this work for additional information regarding copyright ownership.\n * The ASF licenses this file to You under the Apache License, Version 2.0\n * (the \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance with\n * the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *      http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\npackage org.apache.camel.component.fix;\n\nimport org.apache.camel.AsyncCallback;\nimport org.apache.camel.Exchange;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.DefaultAsyncProducer;\nimport org.slf4j.Logger;\nimport org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;\nimport quickfix.Message;\nimport quickfix.Session;\nimport quickfix.SessionID;\n\n/**\n * FIX producer that sends outbound FIX messages from Camel exchanges.\n */\npublic class FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixProducer.class);\n\n    public FixProducer(FixEndpoint endpoint) {\n        super(endpoint);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixEndpoint getEndpoint() {\n        return (FixEndpoint) super.getEndpoint();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        try {\n            Message message = exchange.getIn().getBody(Message.class);\n            if (message == null) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Exchange body must be a quickfix.Message instance\");\n            }\n\n            String sessionIdStr = getEndpoint().getSessionID();\n            SessionID sessionID;\n            if (sessionIdStr != null && !sessionIdStr.isEmpty()) {\n                sessionID = new SessionID(sessionIdStr);\n            } else {\n                // Try to derive SessionID from message headers\n                String senderCompID = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, String.class);\n                String targetCompID = exchange.getIn().getHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, String.class);\n                String fixVersion = getEndpoint().getConfiguration().getFixVersion();\n                if (senderCompID != null && targetCompID != null) {\n                    sessionID = new SessionID(fixVersion, senderCompID, targetCompID);\n                } else {\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\n                            \"Cannot determine FIX session: no sessionID configured and no sender/target comp IDs in headers\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            LOG.debug(\"Sending FIX message to session {}: {}\", sessionID, message);\n\n            Session session = Session.lookupSession(sessionID);\n            if (session == null) {\n                throw new IllegalStateException(\"No FIX session found for session ID: \" + sessionID);\n            }\n\n            boolean sent = session.send(message);\n            if (!sent) {\n                throw new IllegalStateException(\"Failed to send FIX message to session: \" + sessionID);\n            }\n\n            LOG.debug(\"FIX message sent successfully to session: {}\", sessionID);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            exchange.setException(e);\n        }\n        callback.done(true);\n        return true;\n    }\n}\n",

Receives inbound FIX messages via `onMessage(Message, SessionID)`, creates Camel Exchange with message body and header constants, and routes through processor.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixProducer.java (new)\nExtends `DefaultAsyncProducer`. Implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)`. Extracts `quickfix.Message` from exchange body, resolves `SessionID` from configuration or headers, looks up the FIX `Session`, and sends the message.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix (new)\n```\nclass=org.apache.camel.component.fix.FixComponent\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe `camel-fix` component is implemented as a new, clean FIX protocol component for Apache Camel that follows the exact same conventions as the existing `camel-quickfix` component but with a simplified, more direct API.\n\n**Architecture decisions:**\n\n1. **Extends `DefaultComponent`**: The `FixComponent` extends `DefaultComponent` as required, uses the `@Component(\"fix\")` annotation for service discovery via Camel's SPI mechanism. The component creates `FixEndpoint` instances by parsing the URI's `remaining` part as the session ID.\n\n2. **Extends `DefaultEndpoint`**: The `FixEndpoint` uses `@UriEndpoint` with `scheme = \"fix\"` and `syntax = \"fix:sessionID\"`. It stores a `FixConfiguration` instance for endpoint-level parameters. The URI path parameter is the session ID.\n\n3. **Extends `DefaultConsumer`**: The `FixConsumer` provides `onMessage(Message, SessionID)` as the entry point for inbound FIX messages. It creates Camel `Exchange` objects populated with the FIX message body and relevant headers (`CamelFixMessageType`, `CamelFixSessionID`, `CamelFixSenderCompID`, `CamelFixTargetCompID`).\n\n4. **Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`**: The `FixProducer` implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` as required by the task. It extracts `quickfix.Message` from the exchange body and resolves the target `SessionID` either from the endpoint configuration or from message headers. It uses `Session.lookupSession()` from QuickFIX/J to find the active session.\n\n5. **`FixConfiguration` with `@UriParams`**: The configuration POJO groups all URI parameters. Fields include `configFile`, `senderCompID`, `targetCompID`, `fixVersion` (default \"FIX.4.2\"), `heartBeatInterval` (default 30 seconds), `socketConnectHost`, and `socketConnectPort`.\n\n6. **`FixConstants` as header constants**: String constants following Camel's `CamelXxx` naming convention for all FIX-related message headers.\n\n### Integration with Parent Build\n\n- `components/pom.xml` updated to include `<module>camel-fix</module>` in alphabetical order between `camel-file-watch` and `camel-flatpack`\n- `camel-fix/pom.xml` inherits from the `components` parent POM and declares QuickFIX/J dependencies using the `${quickfixj-version}` property defined in the parent\n- The service descriptor file at `META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix` enables Camel's service loader to discover the component by scheme name \"fix\"\n\n### Dependencies\n\nThe component depends on:\n- `camel-support`: Provides `DefaultComponent`, `DefaultEndpoint`, `DefaultConsumer`, `DefaultAsyncProducer` base classes\n- `quickfixj-core`: QuickFIX/J core library for FIX protocol support (`Session`, `SessionID`, `Message`)\n- `quickfixj-messages-all`: All FIX message type definitions\n",

Receives inbound FIX messages via `onMessage(Message, SessionID)`, creates Camel Exchange with message body and header constants, and routes through processor.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixProducer.java (new)\nExtends `DefaultAsyncProducer`. Implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)`. Extracts `quickfix.Message` from exchange body, resolves `SessionID` from configuration or headers, looks up the FIX `Session`, and sends the message.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix (new)\n```\nclass=org.apache.camel.component.fix.FixComponent\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe `camel-fix` component is implemented as a new, clean FIX protocol component for Apache Camel that follows the exact same conventions as the existing `camel-quickfix` component but with a simplified, more direct API.\n\n**Architecture decisions:**\n\n1. **Extends `DefaultComponent`**: The `FixComponent` extends `DefaultComponent` as required, uses the `@Component(\"fix\")` annotation for service discovery via Camel's SPI mechanism. The component creates `FixEndpoint` instances by parsing the URI's `remaining` part as the session ID.\n\n2. **Extends `DefaultEndpoint`**: The `FixEndpoint` uses `@UriEndpoint` with `scheme = \"fix\"` and `syntax = \"fix:sessionID\"`. It stores a `FixConfiguration` instance for endpoint-level parameters. The URI path parameter is the session ID.\n\n3. **Extends `DefaultConsumer`**: The `FixConsumer` provides `onMessage(Message, SessionID)` as the entry point for inbound FIX messages. It creates Camel `Exchange` objects populated with the FIX message body and relevant headers (`CamelFixMessageType`, `CamelFixSessionID`, `CamelFixSenderCompID`, `CamelFixTargetCompID`).\n\n4. **Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`**: The `FixProducer` implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` as required by the task. It extracts `quickfix.Message` from the exchange body and resolves the target `SessionID` either from the endpoint configuration or from message headers. It uses `Session.lookupSession()` from QuickFIX/J to find the active session.\n\n5. **`FixConfiguration` with `@UriParams`**: The configuration POJO groups all URI parameters. Fields include `configFile`, `senderCompID`, `targetCompID`, `fixVersion` (default \"FIX.4.2\"), `heartBeatInterval` (default 30 seconds), `socketConnectHost`, and `socketConnectPort`.\n\n6. **`FixConstants` as header constants**: String constants following Camel's `CamelXxx` naming convention for all FIX-related message headers.\n\n### Integration with Parent Build\n\n- `components/pom.xml` updated to include `<module>camel-fix</module>` in alphabetical order between `camel-file-watch` and `camel-flatpack`\n- `camel-fix/pom.xml` inherits from the `components` parent POM and declares QuickFIX/J dependencies using the `${quickfixj-version}` property defined in the parent\n- The service descriptor file at `META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix` enables Camel's service loader to discover the component by scheme name \"fix\"\n\n### Dependencies\n\nThe component depends on:\n- `camel-support`: Provides `DefaultComponent`, `DefaultEndpoint`, `DefaultConsumer`, `DefaultAsyncProducer` base classes\n- `quickfixj-core`: QuickFIX/J core library for FIX protocol support (`Session`, `SessionID`, `Message`)\n- `quickfixj-messages-all`: All FIX message type definitions\n",

package org.apache.camel.component.fix;

import java.util.Map;

import org.apache.camel.CamelContext;
import org.apache.camel.Endpoint;
import org.apache.camel.spi.annotations.Component;
import org.apache.camel.support.DefaultComponent;

/**
 * FIX (Financial Information eXchange) protocol component for Apache Camel.
 */
@Component("fix")
public class FixComponent extends DefaultComponent {

    public FixComponent() {
    }

    public FixComponent(CamelContext context) {
        super(context);
    }

    @Override
    protected Endpoint createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters) throws Exception {
        FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();
        setProperties(configuration, parameters);

        FixEndpoint endpoint = new FixEndpoint(uri, this, configuration);
        endpoint.setSessionID(remaining);
        setProperties(endpoint, parameters);

        return endpoint;
    }
}
